\'pnpm install\',\n    \'pnpm db:setup\',\n    \'pnpm db:migrate\',\n    \'pnpm db:seed\',\n    \'pnpm dev \',\n  ];\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const timer = setTimeout(() => {\n
